    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (proj_fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(

Model_VideoSumm(
  (proj_fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (proj_fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_text_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_text_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (causal_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (spurious_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
)

  )

        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )

      (ffn_text): FFN(

        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )

  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)

    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)

  )

Model_VideoSumm(
  (proj_fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (proj_fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_text_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_text_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (causal_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (spurious_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
)

Model_VideoSumm(
  (proj_fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (proj_fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_text_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_text_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (causal_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (spurious_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (diff_causal_attribution): DifferentiableCausalAttribution(
    (importance_scorer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
      (1): LayerNorm((64,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (2): ReLU()
      (3): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
      (4): Linear(in_features=64, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
    (intervention_strength): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=32, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=32, out_features=1, bias=True)
      (3): Sigmoid()
    )
    (effect_aggregator): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=128, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
  )
)

    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )

    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(

Model_VideoSumm(
  (proj_fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (proj_fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_text_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_text_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (causal_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (spurious_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (diff_causal_attribution): DifferentiableCausalAttribution(
    (importance_scorer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
      (1): LayerNorm((64,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (2): ReLU()
      (3): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
      (4): Linear(in_features=64, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
    (intervention_strength): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=32, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=32, out_features=1, bias=True)
      (3): Sigmoid()
    )
    (effect_aggregator): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=128, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
  )
)

Model_VideoSumm(
  (proj_fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (proj_fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
  )
  (multiway_list): ModuleList(
    (0-1): 2 x MultiWayTransformer(
      (norm1_fused): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (attn_fusion): MultiHeadAttention(q_dims=128, k_dims=128, v_dims=128, h_dims=128, o_dims=128, heads=8, p=0.5, bias=True)
      (norm2_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_video): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
      (norm2_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (ffn_text): FFN(
        (fc1): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=512, bias=True)
        (act): GELU(approximate='none')
        (drop1): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
        (fc2): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=128, bias=True)
        (drop2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
      )
    )
  )
  (norm_video): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (norm_text): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  (fc_video): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_video_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_video_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_video_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text): Sequential(
    (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=128, bias=True)
    (1): ReLU(inplace=True)
    (2): Dropout(p=0.5, inplace=False)
    (3): LayerNorm((128,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
  )
  (fc_text_cls): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (fc_text_loc): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=2, bias=True)
  (fc_text_ctr): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
  (causal_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (spurious_feature_head): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
  (diff_causal_attribution): DifferentiableCausalAttribution(
    (importance_scorer): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=64, bias=True)
      (1): LayerNorm((64,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (2): ReLU()
      (3): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
      (4): Linear(in_features=64, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
    (intervention_strength): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=32, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=32, out_features=1, bias=True)
      (3): Sigmoid()
    )
    (effect_aggregator): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=128, bias=True)
      (1): ReLU()
      (2): Linear(in_features=128, out_features=1, bias=True)
    )
  )
)
